**[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)加入四逆内，益气固脱救阴伤，**

**病仍不解烦躁者，参苓增来有奇长。**

**[四逆汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx05-0.3.0.0.0.md)中除[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[葱白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.14.0.0.md)加入散寒良。**

**阴盛格阳面见赤，尿胆加进白通汤。**

**四逆加入良桂夏，浆水入煎挽亡阳。**

**阴盛格阳**  指体内阴寒过盛，阳气被拒于外，出现假热的证候。 **亡阳** 临床可见汗出如珠，四肢逆冷、面色苍白、呼吸微弱、脉微欲绝等危象。

本方由[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)等三味药组成。功能救逆回阳。主治恶寒、四肢厥冷、腹痛、吐利、脉沉等症。

本方加[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，名四逆加[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)汤。功能益气阴而固虚脱，主治恶寒、四肢厥冷、下利不禁而脉微欲绝者。

本方加[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，名[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[四逆汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx05-0.3.0.0.0.md)，主治恶寒肢冷、困沉欲睡、烦躁更甚者。

本方去[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，加[葱白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.14.0.0.md)，名白通汤。主治恶寒、四肢冷、下利，脉微者；若再加人尿、猪胆汁，名白通加猪胆汁汤。主治阴盛格阳、面赤、利不止、厥逆、干呕、脉一时伏而不出者。

本方加良姜、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，名浆水散。主治暴泻如水、大汗淋漓、肤冷、脉微之亡阳证。

**6.回阳救急汤**(附: 正阳散、大顺散)

**回阳救急用六君，桂附[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)五味群，**

**加麝三厘或胆汁，三阴寒厥建奇勋。**

**正阳散内仅附姜，甘麝皂荚阴寒伤。**

**大顺散中甘杏桂，霍乱呕吐是妙方。**

本方由六君子汤([人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md))[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)等十味药组成。临服时可根据病情加入[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)或猪胆汁。功能回阳救逆、益气生脉。主治恶寒倦卧、四肢逆冷、吐泻交作等证。

正阳散由[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)、皂荚等五味药组成。主治面青身冷、张口出气、舌黑多唾等阴寒急证。

大顺散由[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)等三味药组成。主治霍乱肢冷吐泻。

**7.参附汤**(附:芪附汤、术附汤)

**参附汤是救急方，补气回阳效力彰，**

**正气大亏阳暴脱，喘汗肢冷可煎尝。**

**除参易芪或易术，芪附术附均高强。**

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)等二味药组成。功能补气回阳。主治正气大亏、阳气暴脱出现的额汗喘急、手足逆冷等亡阳危证。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，加[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)，名芪附汤。主治盗汗。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、加[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，名术附汤。治寒湿身痛。

**8.黑锡丹**

**黑锡丹能镇浮阳，金铃桂附蔻硫黄，**

**芦巴起纸茴沉木，[定喘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.2.2.0.md)痰逆有专长。**

**浮阳**   指肾阳奔浮于上，产生面赤喘促之证。

本方由黑锡、金铃子([川楝子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.12.0.0.md))、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[肉豆蔻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.6.0.0.md)、硫黄、[胡芦巴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.13.0.0.md)、[阳起石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.20.0.0.md)、[破故纸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.8.0.0.md)、[茴香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.9.0.0.0.md)、[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)等十二味药组成。功能镇纳浮阳，主治肾气上浮、气喘、汗出、肢冷等证。

**9.真武汤**

**真武汤壮肾中阳，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)术芍附[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，**

**少阴腹痛寒水气，悸眩瞤惕保安康。**

**瞤**  run，读润(阳平)。形容肌肤抽缩跳动。  **惕** 恐惧。

本方由[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、芍药、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能温肾利水。主治恶寒肢冷腹痛及心悸、头眩、身瞤惕等症。

**10.[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤**(附：[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤)

**少阴阳虚[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)苓芍术堪尝。**

**体痛背寒肢逆冷，脉微无力服之康。**

**[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)草枣姜，体痛脉虚风湿方。**

**去桂加术余减半，风湿伤气效亦良。**

**又有[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤，汗出气短宜煎尝。**

**[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)桂[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，身寒微肿辨端详。**

本方由[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、芍药、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能温经扶阳。主治身体痛、背恶寒、四肢逆冷、脉微无力等症。

[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤由[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等五味药组成。主治风湿病，身体疼痛，不能转侧，大便溏、小便不利者。

[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤即[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤去[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，加[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，主治同上，而大小便正常者。

[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)汤由[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)等四味药组成。主治风湿病，骨节疼痛、不能屈伸、汗出短气，身寒微肿、小便不利者。

### [**其他**]

**11.暖培卑监法**(《时病论》)

**暖培卑监四君强，喜升[葛根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.8.0.0.md)喜燥苍，**

**温以益智缓粳米，土寒泄利炭炮姜。**

**卑监**  土不及为卑监。亦即脾虚。

本方由[四君子汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.1.0.0.0.md)([党参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、白[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md))加[葛根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.8.0.0.md)、[苍术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.2.0.0.md)、益智、粳米、炮姜等组合而成。功能温补脾阳。主治虚寒泄泻及冷痢。

**12.[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)温中汤**

**[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)温中陈草苓，[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)草蔻[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)并，**

**煎服加姜治腹痛，虚寒胀满用皆灵。**

本方由[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、草蔻、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能温中理气。主治虚寒腹胀、服痛等症。

**13.[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[四逆汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx05-0.3.0.0.0.md)**(附:[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)四逆加[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)汤)

**[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)四逆芍[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)甘枣[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)施，**

**内有久寒姜茱入，散寒温里此方宜。**

本方由[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、芍药、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等七味药组成。功能温经散寒，主治恶寒、手足逆冷、脉细欲绝者。亦可用之治冻疮。内有陈寒者，加吴萸、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，名[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)四逆加吴萸[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)汤。

**14.[四神丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx13-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**四神故纸[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)，肉蔻除油五味须，**

**[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)百枚姜八两，五更肾泻火衰扶。**

**五更肾泻**  五更，天快亮时。肾阳虚衰，多天快亮时作泻，故名。

本方由[破故纸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.8.0.0.md)、[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)、[肉豆蔻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.6.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等六味药组成。功能温肾止泻。主治五更作泻。

**15.半硫丸**

**半硫丸内药无多，阳虚气寒便闭疴。**

**或是便溏经日久，此方即可令调和。**

本方由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、硫黄等二味药组成。功能温肾逐寒。主治老年阳虚便秘，或长期大便溏泻不愈。

## 10消导化积剂

###  [**消食导滞**]

**1.[保和丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx06-0.1.0.0.0.md)**(附:大安丸、小[保和丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx06-0.1.0.0.0.md))

保和[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)与[山楂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.1.0.0.md)，苓夏陈翘菔子加，

炊饼为丸白汤下，方中亦可用[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)。

大安丸内加[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，消中兼补效堪夸，

去夏菔翘加术芍，小[保和丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx06-0.1.0.0.0.md)助脾佳。

本方由[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[山楂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、菜服子等七味药组成，方中亦可加[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)，或用[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)汤送下。功能消积和胃。主治食积停滞之腹满时痛、嗳腐吞酸。

本方加[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，名保安丸。功能消而兼补，治脾虚食滞之腹满痛及小儿泄泻。

本方去[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[莱菔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.6.0.0.md)子、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)，加[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)，名小[保和丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx06-0.1.0.0.0.md)。能助脾进食。

**2.[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)导滞丸**(附:[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)导滞九)

**[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)导滞首[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，芩连曲术[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)襄，**

**[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)蒸饼糊丸服，湿热枳滞力能攘。**

**若还后重兼气滞，[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)导滞加[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)。**

本方由[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能消积滞、利湿热。主治舌苔黄腻、胸脘痞满厌食下痢等证。

本方加[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)，名[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)导滞丸。主治湿热痢疾里急后重兼气滞腹胀者。

**3.[木香槟榔丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx06-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)青[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)，枳柏[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)莪术随，**

**[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)黑丑兼[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)，泻痢食疟用咸宜。**

**食疟**  疟疾的一种，乃疟疾兼有食积之证。

本方由[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、莪术、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、黑丑([牵牛子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.3.6.0.0.md))、[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)等十一味药组成。功能行气导滞。主治疟疾兼有脘腹胀满、大便秘结，或赤白痢疾。

**4.枳术丸**(附:曲麦枳术丸、橘半枳术丸、香砂枳术丸)

**枳术丸是消补方，[荷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.15.0.0.md)裹饭为丸良。**

**若于本方加曲麦，食多胀满效尤强。**

**或加[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)与[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，脾虚停痰力能匡。**

**更有方中加香砂，行气消食开胃长。**

本方由[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)二味，以[荷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.15.0.0.md)裹，烧饭而成。功能健脾消胀，主治脾虚食滞引起的腹胀。

本方加[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)，名曲麦枳术丸。治过食不化心腹胀满。

本方加[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、名橘半枳术丸。治脾虚停痰饭食不消、脘腹痞闷。

本方加[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，名香砂枳术丸。功能行气、消食，治宿食不消、气滞胀满。

**5.健脾丸**(附：启脾散)

**健脾参术苓草陈，肉蔻香连合[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，**

**楂肉[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)曲麦炒，消补兼施建奇勋。**

**启脾散中用参术，砂陈莲查五谷虫，**

**脾虚胃弱正可服，疳疾等证妙通神。**

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、肉蔻、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[山楂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.1.0.0.md)肉、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)等十三味药组成。功能补脾消食。主治脾虚食停，食纳减退，脘腹胀满、大便稀溏等症。

启脾散由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、莲肉、[山楂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.1.0.0.md)炭、五谷虫等七味药组成。主治脾胃虚弱，食少形瘦，渐成疳积。

### [**消痞化积**]

**6.[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)消痞丸**

**[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)消痞四君全，麦夏与曲朴姜连，**

**消积除满兼清热，消中有补两相兼。**

本方由[四君子汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.1.0.0.0.md)([人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md))加[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)曲、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)曲、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)等九味药组成。功能补脾消积。主治脾虚食积，心下痞满，食欲不振。

**7.葛花解酲汤**

**葛花解酲香[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，参术蔻青陈二苓，**

**[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)兼[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)，温中化湿酒醉灵。**

酲 chéng，读成，因酒致病为醒。

本方由葛花、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[白豆蔻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[猪苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)等十三味药组成。功能温中化湿。主治饮多伤脾，眩晕呕吐、胸膈痞闷。

**8.蟾砂散**

**蟾砂散用大[蟾蜍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.13.0.0.0.md)，[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)纳腹泥封涂，**

**煅红研末桔汤下，气臌得此数服除。**

本方由[蟾蜍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.13.0.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)等二味药组成。功能行气消积。主治气臌，并治小儿疳积、面黄肌瘦，肚腹胀满。

**9.[鳖甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.15.0.0.md)煎丸**(附:化（疒征）回生开)

**[鳖甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.15.0.0.md)煎丸疟母方，䗪虫鼠妇及蜣螂，**

**蜂窠[石苇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.11.0.0.md)硝黄射，桂朴凌霄丹芍姜，**

**[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)柴芩阿[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)葶劳和参尝。**

**化（疒征）回生苏子霜，艾蒲椒炭桂参香，**

**杏桃归芍萸芎索，[苏木](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.18.0.0.md)[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)片子姜，**

**虻蛭良脂棱乳没，降香茴麝与[丁香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.8.0.0.0.md)，**

**两头尖漆真[阿魏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.22.0.0.0.md)，益母鳖胶地[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，**

**寒邪侵袭深延入，血分成（疒征）证可详，**

**炼蜜为丸钱五重，蜡皮封护慎毋忘。**

**疟母**   指疟疾日久不愈，协下有块。

本方由䗪虫、鼠妇(地虱婆)、蜣螂、蜂房、[鳖甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.15.0.0.md)、[石苇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.11.0.0.md)、赤硝、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[射干](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.11.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[凌霄花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.24.0.0.md)、牡丹、芍药、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)、葶苈、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)等二十三味药组成。功能消（疒征）化积。主治疟母。

化（疒征）回生丹由苏子霜、[艾叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.15.0.0.md)炭、[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)炭、[川椒](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.7.0.0.0.md)炭、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)尾、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)、川芎、[延胡索](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[苏木](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.18.0.0.md)、[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)、片子[姜黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.4.0.0.md)、虻虫、水蛭、良姜、[五灵脂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.22.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、降香、小[茴香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.9.0.0.0.md)炭、[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[丁香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.8.0.0.0.md)、两头尖(竹节[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md))、[干漆](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.27.0.0.md)、真[阿魏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.22.0.0.0.md)、益母膏、[鳖甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.15.0.0.md)胶、地黄、三棱、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)等三十五味药组成、炼蜜为丸，重一钱五分、蜡皮封护。功能逐淤散结，消（疒征）化积。主治寒邪入里，日久血凝成淤，结成（疒征）积。及妇人经闭、干血痨等症。 

**10.胆道排石汤**(天津南开医院验方)

**胆道排石[郁金](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.3.0.0.md)香，[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)与[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，**

**金钱草同[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)配，或制丸剂缓缓尝。**

本方由[郁金](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、金钱草、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)等六味药组成。功能清热利湿、行气止痛。主治胆石症。

**11.海藻玉壶汤**(《医宗金鉴·外科心法要诀》)

**海藻玉壶藻带昆，[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)半贝与青陈，**

**川芎[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)合，化痰散结善消瘿。**

本方由海藻、[昆布](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.14.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、浙贝、[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、川芎、[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)等十味药组成。功能化痰散结。主治瘿瘤(颈项及腋窝结核如李如桃)。

## 11补益剂

### [**补气**]

**1.[四君子汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.1.0.0.0.md)**(附:六君子汤，异功散、香砂六君子汤、六散神)。

[四君子汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.1.0.0.0.md)中和义，参术[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)比。

益以夏陈名六君，祛痰补气阳虚饵。

除却[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)名异功，或加香砂胃寒使。

加入豆芪名六神，脾虚食少虚热宜。

**饵** ěr， 读耳，食用、服用。

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等四味药组成。功能补脾益气。主治脾胃虚弱，食少无力，面白声微，便溏等症。

本方加[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)，名六君子汤，功能补气祛痰，主治脾胃气虚，饮食不思，呕吐吞酸等症。六君去[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，名异功散，主治脾虚呕吐泻泄。

本方加[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，名香砂六君子汤。主治睥胃虚寒呕吐食少。

本方加扁豆、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)，名六神散。主治脾胃虚弱，津气不足，饮食减少，身热乏力等症。

**2.参苓[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)散**(附:资生丸)

**参苓[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)扁豆陈，[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)甘莲砂苡仁，**

**[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)上浮兼保肺，枣汤调服益脾神。**

**资生丸亦参术苓，去枣加藿白蔻仁，**

**橘连泽黄山查麦，调理脾胃力能行。**

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、扁豆、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、莲肉、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、苡仁、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等十二味药组成。功能健脾补气，和胃渗湿。主治四肢乏力，饮食不消，或吐或泻等症。

本方去[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，加[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)、白蔻仁、橘红、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[山楂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[麦芽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[芡实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.12.0.0.md)，名资生丸。主治脾虚兼有舌苔黄腻、尿黄便泄等症。

**3.[补中益气汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**补中益气芪术陈，升柴参草[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)身，**

**劳倦内伤功独擅，亦治阳虚外感因。**

本方由[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能补中益气。主治劳倦伤气、少气懒言、食欲不佳。亦治体虚外感及气虚下陷之脱肛、子宫下垂等证。

**4.[玉屏风散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.12.0.0.0.md)**

**[玉屏风散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.12.0.0.0.md)最有灵，芪术[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)鼎足形，**

**表虚汗多易感冒，药虽相畏效相成。**

**鼎足**  鼎，dǐng，读顶，古代炊器，有三足。在此比喻三药并立。

本方由[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)三味药组成。[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)两药虽相畏，其效相成，三药合用，有益气固表止汗之功能。主治表虚自汗容易感冒。

**5.保元汤**

**保元补益总偏温，桂草参芪四味珍，**

**男妇虚劳幼科痘，阳虚气弱力能振。**

本方由[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)等四味药组成。功能温阳补气。主治虚劳及幼科痘疮顶陷浆清之证。

**6.[生脉散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.9.0.0.0.md)**

**生脉麦味与参施，补气生津保肺机，**

**少气汗多口干渴，病危脉绝效力奇。**

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、麦冬、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)等三味药组成。功能补气生津。主治热伤元气，少气汗多，体倦口渴及久咳肺虚，痰少舌燥等证。本方在病危脉绝时用，尤见功效。

**7.[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[蛤蚧](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.15.0.0.md)散**(附:[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[胡桃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.16.0.0.md)汤)

**宝鉴[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[蛤蚧](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.15.0.0.md)散，喘咳痰血与胸烦，**

**桑皮二母杏苓草，若非虚热慎毋餐。**

**动则喘息不能卧，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[胡桃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.16.0.0.md)[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)揽。**

**宝鉴**  指《卫生宝鉴》

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[蛤蚧](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.15.0.0.md)、[桑白皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.6.0.0.md)、[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能补气清肺，益肾平喘。主治久病喘咳，咳吐壮脓血、胸中烦热等证。对新咳有外邪而非虚热者不能妄用。

[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[胡桃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.16.0.0.md)汤由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[胡桃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.16.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等三味药组成，功能纳气平喘，主治动则喘息，不能平卧。

**8.升阳益胃汤**(《牌胃论》)

**内伤升阳益胃汤，湿多热少抑清阳，**

**倦怠懒食身重病，口苦舌干便不常，**

**六君[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)连[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)，羌独[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)柴与防。**

本方由六君子汤([人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md))[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)等十四味药组成。功能补脾燥湿，益胃升阳。主治倦怠懒食，身重而痛，口苦舌干，大便不调、小便频数等证。

**9.参麦汤**(《湿热病篇》)

**气液两亏宜清补，当推薜氏参麦汤，**

**参麦瓜斛草莲谷，肺气胃津两复方**。

**薜氏** 指清代医学家薜生白。 

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、麦冬、[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[石斛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.4.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、鲜[莲子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.13.0.0.md)、谷芽等七味药组成。功能补气养阴，扶胃益肺。主治气液两亏之倦怠不思食，唇齿干而小便频数等症。

### [**补血**]

**10.[四物汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.3.0.0.0.md)**

**四物地芍与归芎，血家百病此方通，**

**凡属血虚之病证，加减运用在胸中，**

本方由熟地、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、川芎等四味药组成。功能补血调血。主治血虚百病及妇人经水不调，阴道下血诸症。

**11.[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)补血汤**

**[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)补血东垣笺，[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)一两归二钱，**

**证象白虎烦渴甚，脉大而虚宜此煎。**

**东垣笺**  东垣、指元朝著名医学家李东垣。笺，jiān ，读歼，在此指书写方剂的用笺。

本方由[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)等二味药组成。功能补气生血。主治劳倦伤气烦渴欲饮，脉洪大。此虽证象白虎，但烦渴不能饮冷，脉洪大按之必虚。

**12.[归脾汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.4.0.0.0.md)**(附:妙香散)

**[归脾汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.4.0.0.0.md)用术参芪，归草[茯神](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.2.0.0.md)[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)随，**

**酸枣[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)[龙眼肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.7.0.0.md)，煎加姜枣益心脾。**

**妙香散内参芪草，二茯[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)与[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)，**

**辰砂桔麝[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)入，治疗惊怖意不定。**

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[茯神](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[酸枣仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[龙眼肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.7.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等十二味药组成。功能健脾养心，益气生血。主治劳伤心脾，怔仲健忘、食少不眠。亦治妇人脾虚月经不尽。

妙香散由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[茯神](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[朱砂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)等十一味药组成。主治心气不足，惊悸恐怖、虚烦少睡、饮食无味，心神不宁等证。

**13.[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)[羊肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.22.0.0.md)汤**(附:[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[羊肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.22.0.0.md)汤)

**[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)[羊肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.22.0.0.md)汤，产后腹痛蓐劳匡，**

**虚劳寒疝皆堪治，痛呕[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)襄。**

**更有[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[羊肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.22.0.0.md)汤，参芪加入是其方，**

**产后发热自汗出，肢体疼痛服之良。**

**蓐劳**  蓐rǔ，读蓐， 蓐劳，病名。因产后感受风寒所致。症见寒热如疟，肢体倦怠，咳嗽气逆等症。 

本方由[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[羊肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.22.0.0.md)等三味药组成。功能温中补血，祛寒止痛。主治产后蓐劳腹痛及虚劳寒疝腹痛，若痛多而呕者，加[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)。

本方加[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)，名[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[羊肉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.22.0.0.md)汤，治产后发热自汗，肢体疼痛。

**14.复脉汤**(附:加减复脉汤)

**复脉[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)参桂姜，麦冬生地麻仁襄，**

**[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)加酒服，虚劳肺痿效力强。**

**除去参桂[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)姜，加入[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)治阴伤，**

**温邪久羁阳明证，身热口干服之康。**

木方由[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、麦冬、生地、麻仁、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)、[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)等九味药加酒、水煎煮而成。功能养阴复脉。主治虚劳及肺痿病。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，加[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)，名加减复脉汤。治温邪久留，身热口干、面赤舌燥、脉虚大者。(路振平)

###  [**气血两补**]

**15.八珍汤**(附:十全大补汤、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)养营汤、[泰山磐石散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx18-0.4.0.0.0.md))

**四君四物八珍汤，气血两补是名方。**

**再加[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)与[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)，十全大补效无双。**

**若益志陈[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)，去芎辛窜养营良。**

**十全汤内去茯桂，加续芩砂磐石强。**

窜cuàn，读篡，乱跑。 磐pán，读盘，大石头。

本方由[党参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、川芎、熟地、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)八味药组成。功能气血双补。主治气血两虚的病证。

本方加[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)，名十全大补汤，较原方补益功效更好。

本方减去辛香走窜的川芎，加[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)，[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)，名[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)养营汤，功能温补气血，安神和胃，主治气血两虚所致的心悸、健忘、失眠、食少、乏力等证。

原方去[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)，加[续断](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.xd.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，叫[泰山磐石散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx18-0.4.0.0.0.md)，功能补气、养血、安胎，主治妇人气血两虚，倦怠少食，有坠胎先兆者。

**16.薯蓣丸**

**薯蓣丸中用八珍，桔防豆枣阿[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)，**

**桂姜麦蔹同柴曲，风气虚劳总可珍。**

**风气**  此处泛指病邪。

本方是八珍汤加[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、大豆卷、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)、[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、麦冬、[白蔹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.14.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)、[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)等十二味药组成。功能健脾益胃，扶正祛邪。用于劳伤所致的慢性衰弱性疾病。

### [**补阴**]

**17.[六味地黄丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.5.0.0.0.md)**(附:知柏地黄丸、杞菊地黄丸、都气丸，八仙长寿丸)

**六味地黄益肾肝，茱薯丹泽地苓专。**

**更加知柏成八味，阴虚火旺可煎餐。**

**养阴明目加杞菊，滋[阴都](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.1.7-8-0.0.2.3.19.md)气五味搬，**

**肺肾两调金水生，麦冬加入长寿丸。**

本方由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、山萸肉、干[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)等六味药组成。功能滋阴补肾。主治腰膝瘘弱，烦热咽干等证。

本方加入[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)，名知柏八味丸，功能滋阴补肾，清热泻火，主治骨蒸潮热，虚烦盗汗等证。

本方加[枸杞](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.8.0.0.md)子、菊花，名杞菊地黄丸，功能滋阴养血，养肝明目，主治目晃畏光，视物模糊或枯涩疼痛等证。

本方加入[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)，名都气丸，功能滋阴敛肺，化痰止咳，主治肺虚咳嗽，经久不愈，气促，动则更甚。

本方加麦冬、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)，名八仙长寿丸。功能滋阴敛肺。主治虚劳久咳，潮热盗汗，遗精等证。

**18.左归饮**(附:左归丸)

**左归萸地药苓从，杞草齐成壮水功。**

**若要为丸除苓草，更加龟鹿二胶从，**

**菟丝[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)均采用，精血能充效无穷。**

**虚火上炎阴失守，去除柏鹿益门冬。**

本方由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、山萸肉、干[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[枸杞](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.8.0.0.md)子、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等六味药组成。功能滋阴补肾。主治腰酸遗精，烦热盗汗，口舌干燥等症。

本方减[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，加龟胶、鹿胶、川[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)、[菟丝子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.7.0.0.md)，名左归丸。功能填补肝肾真阴。主治肢冷、腰膝痿弱、精神疲乏、日渐衰弱等证。如肾阴虚而虚火上炎，咽干舌燥，则应去鹿胶再加[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)。

**19.大补阴丸**(附:通关丸)

**大补阴丸治水亏，虚火劳热致虚羸，**

**地黄龟板兼知柏，猪脊髓共蜜和为。**

**滋肾通关桂柏知，溺癃不渴下焦医，**

**丸号通关能利水，又名滋肾补阴虚。**

本方由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、龟板等四味药组成。功能滋阴，主治潮热盗汗，咳嗽咯血，足心热等证。

[滋肾通关丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx04-0.12.0.0.0.md)由[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)等三味药组成。功能滋阴补肾，温化利尿。主治膀胱气化不行所致的小便闭癃。

**20.虎潜丸**

**虎潜足痿是神方，[虎骨](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.11.0.0.md)[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)共[锁阳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.4.0.0.md)，**

**龟板[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)芍，再加柏地制丸尝。**

**潜** qián，读钱，藏。

本方由虎胫骨、[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[锁阳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.4.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、龟板、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)等十味药组成。功能滋阴降火，强筋壮骨。主治肝肾精血不足所致的痿证。

**21.大造丸**

**河车大造地天冬，[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)从，**

**龟板麦冬川[杜仲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.0.md)，阴虚劳伤此方宗。**

**河车**  即[紫河车](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.17.0.0.md)，俗称胞衣。**宗**   zōng 读综，宗师，在此有取法之意。

本方由[紫河车](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.17.0.0.md)、[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)、淡苁蓉、[天门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.3.0.0.md)、盐[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[锁阳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[枸杞](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.8.0.0.md)子、[杜仲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.0.md)、龟板、麦冬等十三味药组成。功能补真元，益精血。凡肝肾不足所致的劳伤虚损诸证，均可取法此方。

**22.[天王补心丹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.11.0.0.0.md)**

**天王补心柏枣仁，二冬生地与[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**三参[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)[朱砂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.1.0.0.md)味，[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)归身共养神。**

本方由柏子仁、[酸枣仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[天门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.3.0.0.md)、[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[干地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[丹参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[远志](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[朱砂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.1.0.0.md)等十四味药组成。功能滋阴清热，养血安神。主治烦热咽干，失眠多梦、

 心悸、健忘等症。

**23.甘麦[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)汤**

**[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[小麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.4.0.0.md)[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)汤，妇人脏臊服之康，**

**精神恍惚悲欲哭，和肝解郁效力彰。**

**脏躁**是一种类似癔病的发作性疾病、以女性为多见。

本方由[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[小麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)三味药物组成。功能养心安神。解郁缓急，主治因忧愁思郁过度所致之脏躁病。

**24.—贯煎**

**[一贯煎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.6.0.0.0.md)中用地黄，[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)杞子麦冬襄，**

**[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)川楝水煎服，肝肾阴虚是妙方。**

**襄** xiang，读香，帮助。

本方由[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、北[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)、[枸杞](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.8.0.0.md)子、[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、川楝等六味药组成。功能滋养肝肾。主治腰痛咽干，肋痛、阴囊肿痛等证。

**25.[酸枣仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.1.0.0.md)汤**

**酸枣二升先煮汤，茯知二两佐之良，**

**芎二甘一相调剂，服后安然入睡乡。**

本方由[酸枣仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、川芎、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能苏血安神，清热除烦。主治虚烦不眠。

**26.拯阴理劳汤（《医宗必读》）**

**阴虚火动用拯阴，皮寒骨蒸咳嗽侵，**

**食少痰多烦少气，生脉归芍地版贞，**

**薏苡橘丹莲合草，汗多不寐加枣仁，**

**燥痰桑贝湿苓半，[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)咳血骨热深。**

本方由[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、蔻苡仁、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、北五味、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[莲子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.13.0.0.md)、橘红、[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等十二味药组成。功能滋阴降火，健脾益气。主治皮面冷而内热如蒸、咳嗽短气、倦怠少气等证。不寐加枣仁；燥痰加桑皮、[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)；湿痰加[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)；骨蒸劳热，咳痰带血加[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)。

**27.[补肺阿胶汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.7.0.0.0.md)（附：月华丸）**

**补肺[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)[马兜铃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.8.0.0.md)，鼠粘[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)杏糯呈，**

**肺虚火盛人当服，顺气生津咳嗽宁。**

**月华丸最能滋阴，二冬二地沙贝苓。**

**药部[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)广[三七](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.12.0.0.md)，獭肝桑菊保肺金。**

**獭**ta，读塔，动物名，水獭。

本方由[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[马兜铃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.8.0.0.md)、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、鼠沽子（[牛蒡子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.2.0.0.md)）、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、糯米等六味药组成。功能补肺止咳。主治肺虚咳嗽，痰粘不易咯出，咽中气梗等证。

月华丸由[天门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.3.0.0.md)、[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[百部](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.5.0.0.md)、川[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、白[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、白菊花、[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)、[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[三七](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.12.0.0.md)、[桑叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.3.0.0.md)、獭肝等十四味药组成。功能滋阴润肺。主治阴虛燥热，久咳不已之肺痨病。

**28.[石斛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.4.0.0.md)夜光丸**

**石斟夜光枳膝芎，二地二冬杞丝苁，**

**青箱草决犀羚药，参味连芩蒺草风。**

本方由[天门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.3.0.0.md)、[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[党参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[石斛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.4.0.0.md)、[枸杞](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.8.0.0.md)子、草决明、青箱子、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)、川芎、[羚羊角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)、川连、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)、苁蓉、[蒺藜子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.7.2.0.0.md)、[菟丝子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.7.0.0.md)、[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)等二十一味药组成。功能平肝清热，滋肾明目。主治头晕目胀，视物昏花。

### [补阳]

**29.肾气丸（附：济生肾气九、十补丸）**

**金匮肾气治肾虚，熟地淮药及山萸，**

**丹皮苓泽加附桂，引火归元热下趋。**

**济生加入车[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)，二便通调肿胀除。**

**若加[鹿茸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.1.0.0.md)[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)，十补丸子肾阳扶。**

**匮** kui，读愧，《金匮》书名。

本方由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[山茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能温肾壮阳，主治腰痛足冷、阳痿、尿频等症。

本方加车前子、[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)，名济生肾气丸，功能温肾利水，主治小便不利，腰重肢冷等症。

本方如加[鹿茸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)，名十补丸，功能温肾壮阳，主治足冷、阳痿、少腹拘急、形体消瘦、小便不利等症。

**30.右归饮（附：右归丸）**

**右归桂附兼[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)，杞子地黄[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)炙，**

**[杜仲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.0.md)山萸煎汤饮，益火之源不可缺。**

**除却[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)鹿胶入，菟丝[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)改丸作。**

本方由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[山茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[枸杞](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.8.0.0.md)子、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[杜仲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.0.md)、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能温肾壮阳，填精补虚。主治腰酸阳瘘，食少便溏等症。

本方去[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，加鹿胶、[菟丝子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.7.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，名右归丸，功能补肾填精，主治年老久病，阳痿遗精等症。

**31.拯阳理劳汤（《医宗必读》）**

**阳虚气弱用拯阳，倦怠恶烦劳则张，**

**表热自汗身酸痛，减去升柴补中方，**

**更添桂味寒加附，泄入升柴诃蔻香，**

**夏咳减桂加麦味，冬咳不减味[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)。**

木方由[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、五味、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等十味药组成。功能助阳益气，补虛理中。主治倦怠懶言，动则气喘，表热自汗。

本方即[补中益气汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.2.0.0.0.md)去[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)，加[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)二味而成，临床运用注意加减变通，寒盛加[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)；泄泻加[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)、[诃子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.7.0.0.md)、白蔻、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)；夏月咳去[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)，加麦冬、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md);冬月咳再加千姜。

**32.升陷汤(《医学衷中参西录》）**

**张氏巧思升陷汤，[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)为君[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)旁，**

**升柴[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)为舟楫，气难接续试此方。**

**楫** ji，读疾，划船用的桨。

本方由[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)，[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)，[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)，[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)，[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能益气升陷。主治气虛下陷，气短不足以息之证。方中以[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)为主药，[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)，[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)，[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)为辅药，协同建功，好象划浆以助船行。

### **【涩肠固脱】**

**3.桃花散（附：[赤石脂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.8.0.0.md)[禹余粮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.9.0.0.md)汤）**

木方由[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)，[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)，龟板，椿根皮，[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)等六味药组成。功能凉血滋明，固崩止带。主治阴虛火旺所致之崩漏。

**11.樗树根丸（附，愈带丸)**

**樗树根丸良姜灰，[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)樗皮[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)随，**

**湿热阻胞成带下，淋漓腥秽此方推。**

**愈带丸中[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)，归芍芎柏椿良姜，**

**妇人冲任带失司，经浊淋漓宜此方。**

**腥** xing，读星，此处指腥气。

本方由良姜，[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)，[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)，樗根皮等四味药组成。功能清热燥湿，固崩止带。主治口苦而渴，带下腥臭，小便黄赤或便溺癃刺痛等证。

本方去樗根皮，加[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，川芎，椿根皮，名愈带丸，功能滋阴止带，主沿赤白带下，淋漓不断之证。

**12.易黄汤(《傅青主女科》〉**

**易黄带下功效奇，[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)[白果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.20.0.0.md)并[芡实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.12.0.0.md)，**

**[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)车前清湿热，一切湿热并能医。**

本方由[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)，[芡实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.12.0.0.md)，[白果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.20.0.0.md)，[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)，车前子等五味药组成。功能健脾利湿，泄热止带。主治下焦湿热所致的黄带。

## 14理气剂

### 【行气】

**1.[越鞠丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx08-0.1.0.0.0.md)**

**[越鞠丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx08-0.1.0.0.0.md)治六郁侵，气血痰火湿食因，**

**芎苍[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)兼栀曲，气畅郁舒痛闷伸。**

**鞠** ju，读居。

本方由[苍术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.2.0.0.md)，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)，川芎，[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)，扼子等五味药组成。功能行气解郁，消积止痛。主治气，血，痰，火，湿，食等郁结所致的胸膈满闷，脘腹胀痛，吞酸呕吐，饮食不化等证。

**2.[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)汤**

**[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)气滞疏，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)共[紫苏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.3.0.0.md)，**

**加枣同煎名四七，痰涎凝聚尽能袪。**

本方由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，苏叶，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能开郁化痰。主治痰气郁结之梅核气。

本方加[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，名四七汤，其健脾祛痰之功尤胜。

**3.加味[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)汤（附：[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)汤）**

**加味[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)汤[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)乌草伦，**

**配入胡索共六味，月经胀痛效堪珍。**

**加入[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)去砂索，专治[血海](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.1.4-6-0.0.1.3.10.md)痛不宁。**

本方由[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)，[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，玄胡索，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等六味药组成、功能行气解郁。主治妇女经期少腹胀痛。

本方加[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，去[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，玄胡索，名[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)汤，功能调经止痛，主治月经不调，经来腹痛。

**4.[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)[薤白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.14.0.0.md)白酒汤**

**瓜蒌[薤白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.14.0.0.md)治胸痹，配以白酒最相宜，**

**加夏加朴枳桂投，治症稍殊名亦导。**

本方由[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)实，[薤白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.14.0.0.md)，白酒等三味药组成。功能通阳散结。主治气滞痰阻之胸痹证。

本方加[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，名[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)[薤白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.14.0.0.md)[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)汤，主治胸痹不得卧，心痛彻背。本方去白酒，加[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)，[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)，名[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)[薤白](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.14.0.0.md)[桂枝汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx01-0.1.0.0.0.md)，功能消痞泄满，主治胸中痞满，气从胁下上逆抢心。

**5.暖肝煎**

**6.[天台乌药散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx08-0.3.0.0.0.md)（附：三层[茴香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.9.0.0.0.md)丸)**

本方去[巴豆](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.3.5.0.0.md)，[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)，良姜，[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)，加[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)，荜拨，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)，名三层[茴香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.9.0.0.0.md)丸，功能温阳散寒，主治脐腹冷痛，寒疝，腹中急痛。
