**9.金铃子散（附：[延胡索](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.2.0.0.md)汤）**

**金铃子散止痛方，须辨作痛多种因，**

**胡索金铃调酒下，制方原是远温辛，**

**[延胡索](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.2.0.0.md)汤七情伤，血气刺痛服之良，**

**归芍乳没香甘桂，胡索[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)黄。**

木方由金铃子，玄胡索两味药组成，功能舒肝止痛，主治肝郁气滞之火痛，时作时止。

[延胡索](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.2.0.0.md)散由玄胡索，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)，赤芍，[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)，[姜黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)，[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)，[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等十味药组成。功能舒肝解郁。主治心腹作痛，上下攻刺，以及妇女月经不调。

**10.[丹参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.7.0.0.md)饮**

**[丹参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.7.0.0.md)饮用大[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)，更入[檀香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.10.0.0.md)妙绝伦，**

**温胃化淤兼理气，胃脘疼痛即舒伸。**

本方由[丹参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.7.0.0.md)，[檀香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.10.0.0.md)，[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)等三味药组成。功能理气止痛。主治气滞血淤所致之心胃气痛。

**11.启膈散**

**启膈散中用[郁金](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.3.0.0.md)，沙丹二参贝荷苓，**

**杵头糠与[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)亮，噎膈津枯劳可饮。**

杵 chu，读除（上声），木棒。

本方由[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)，[丹参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.7.0.0.md)，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，川[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[郁金](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.3.0.0.md)，[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)壳，[荷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.15.0.0.md)蒂，杵头糠等八味药组成。功能润燥解郁，开关进食。主治吞咽困难，噎膈不下。

**12.化肝煎(《景岳全书》）**

**肝郁化火化肝煎，青陈栀泽贝芍丹，**

**气舒郁火自然解，烦热满痛并能安。**

本方由[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)，[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)，梔子，[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)，土[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)，芍药，丹皮等七味药组成。功能疏肝解郁，泄火除烦。主治烦热胁痛、胸闷不舒，脘腹胀满等证。

### 【降气】

**13.[旋复代赭汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx08-0.4.0.0.0.md)**

**旋复代赭用[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)姜甘[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)增，**

**噫气不除心下痞，虚中实证此方灵。**

噫 yi，读衣，噫气，指胃气上逆。

本方由旋复花，[代赭石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等七味药组成。功能降逆和胃，主治心下痞满、噫气不止，以及反胃呕吐等症。

**14.橘皮[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)汤（附：济生橘皮竹茄汤、新制橘皮[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)汤〉**

**橘皮[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)治呕呃，参甘姜枣效力捷，**

**严氏济生方名同，加苓夏麦[枇杷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.9.0.0.md)。**

**新制橘皮[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)汤，亦止吐逆与呕呃，**

**去参枣草加柿蒂，鞠通立法疗胃热。**

本方由橘皮，[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)，[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等六味药组成、功能补中降逆。主治胃虚有热所致之呕吐呃逆等症。

本方加[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，麦冬，[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[枇杷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.9.0.0.md)，名济生橘皮[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)汤，功能养阴清胃，主治口渴，呕吐，呃逆，不食等症。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，加柿蒂，名新制橘皮[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)汤，功降能逆止呃、主治胃热呃逆等症。

**15.[丁香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.8.0.0.0.md)柿蒂汤（附：柿蒂汤、柿钱散）**

**[丁香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.8.0.0.0.md)柿蒂[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)姜，呃逆因寒中气戕，**

**济生参去仅三味，呃逆不止胸满尝。**

**柿钱散去[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)用，专治呃逆名亦彰。**

戕 giang，读枪，损害。

本方由[丁香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.8.0.0.0.md)，柿蒂，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等四味药组成。功能温中止呃。主治呃逆、呕吐、脘闷胸痞等症。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md).，名济生柿蒂汤，功能温胃降逆，主治胸脘满闷，呃逆不止等症。

**16.大[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)汤（附：小[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)汤、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)丸）**

**大[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)汤治胃反，朝食暮吐急须挽，**

**[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)白蜜共三味，降逆培中法当赞。**

**除去参蜜加[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，支饮呕吐不渴鉴。**

**仅去白蜜易[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)，妊娠呕吐治不难。**

本方由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，白蜜三味药组成。功能降气润下。主治朝食暮吐，咽干便结之反胃证。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，白蜜，加[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，名小[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)汤，功能和胃散饮，主治呕吐涎沫，口不渴。

本方去白蜜加[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)，名[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)丸，功能温中降逆，主治妊娠呕吐不止和寒性呕吐。

**17.四磨饮（附：五磨饮子）**

**四磨饮治七情侵，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)及槟沉，**

**四味浓磨煎温服，实邪[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)易[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)。**

**去参加入[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)枳，五磨饮子白酒斟。**

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)，[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)，[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)等四味药组成。功能降气开郁。主治上气喘急，胸脘满闷等症。

本方去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，加[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)，以白酒磨服，名五磨饮子，功能破滞宽中，主治胸闷不舒，时作暧气之证。

**18.[定喘汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx12-0.4.0.0.0.md)**

**[定喘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.2.2.0.md)[白果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.20.0.0.md)与[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)，款冬[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)白皮桑，**

**杏苏[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)兼[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，膈肺寒热喘哮尝。**

木方由[白果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.20.0.0.md)，[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)，苏子，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[款冬花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.4.0.0.md)，[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)，[桑白皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.6.0.0.md)，[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)，[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)等九味药组成。功能宣肺[定喘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.2.2.0.md)。主治风寒外束，痰热内蕴之哮喘证。

**19.苏子降气汤**

**苏子降气橘半归，[前胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.1.0.0.md)桂朴草姜依，**

**下虚上盛痰嗽喘，或入[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)贵合机。**

本方由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，苏子，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)，[前胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.1.0.0.md)，[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)，[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等九味药组成。功能降逆平喘，温化寒痰。主治痰涎壅盛，咳喘短气，胸膈满闷，不时发作。

本方加[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)，则降气之力更增。

## 15理血剂

### 【活血祛淤】

**1.[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)承气汤（附[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)散)**

**[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)承气五般施，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)硝黄并[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，**

**热结膀胱小腹胀，如狂蓄血最相宜。**

**[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)散用䗪虫奇，桂茯苡膝赭黄围。**

**主治经来脐腹痛，寒热如疟勿迟疑。**

本方由[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[芒硝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.2.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能破血逐淤，主治蓄血，少腹急结，其人如狂，小便自利，以及血淤经闭、行经疼痛。

[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)散由[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，䗪虫，[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)心，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)，[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)，[代赭石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能行淤止痛。主治来经绕脐腹痛，寒热似疟等症。

**2.抵当汤（附：抵当丸、下淤血汤）**

**抵当直抵当攻处，[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)蛭虻[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)聚。**

**专治蓄血且发狂，淤血下行病自去**

**改汤为丸属缓剂，病勿急逐正可取。**

**仅用䗪虫配桃黄，主治妇人血着脐。**

本方由[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，水蛭，虻虫等四味药组成，功能逐淤通便。主治少腹硬满，小便自利，其人发狂，以及妇人经闭少腹硬满而拒按之蓄血重症，如病情较轻，可将汤剂改为丸剂从缓图治。

原方去水蛭，虻虫，加䗪虫，名下淤血汤，功能破血下淤，主治产妇因干血内结，著于脐下而致腹痛，亦治血淤而致经水不畅之证。

**3.[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)䗪虫丸**

**[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)䗪虫苓芍桃，地黄杏草漆蛴螬，**

**虻虫水蛭和丸服，淤去新生此剂豪。**

本方由[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)，赤芍药，[干地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[干漆](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.27.0.0.md)，虻虫，水蛭，蛴螬，䗪虫等十二味药组成。功能逐淤生新。主治虚劳消瘦，腹满不食，肌肤甲错等症。

**4.[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)丸**

**仲景[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)丸，丹芍[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)共五般，**

**等分炼蜜和丸服，活血化淤癥块蠲。**

本方由[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，丹皮，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，赤芍药等五味药组成。功能化淤消癥。主治妇人少腹宿有癥块，挛急作痛，亦治妇女经闭，腹痛拒按。

**5.[温经汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx18-0.1.0.0.0.md)（附：艾附暖宫丸）**

**温经归芍桂萸芎，姜夏丹皮又麦冬，**

**参草扶脾胶益血，调经亦可法崩中。**

**艾附暖宫用四物，吴萸[续断](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.xd.md)与桂芪，**

**米醋糊丸醋汤下，妇人子宫虚冷宜。**

本方由[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，芍药，川芎，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)，丹皮，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，麦冬等十二味药组成。功能温经祛淤。主治月经不调，或前或后，经来腹痛，或久不受孕。

艾附暖宫丸由[艾叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.15.0.0.md)、香[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)，[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)，川芎，[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)，[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)，官桂等九味药组成。功能养血温经。主治子宫虚寒，少腹冷、月经过多或淋漓不尽。

**6.[生化汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx18-0.5.0.0.0.md)（附：黑神散)**

**[生化汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx18-0.5.0.0.0.md)宜产后尝，归芎桃草炮姜良，**

**消淤活血功偏擅，止痛温经效亦强。**

**黑神散中有熟地，归芍[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)桂炮姜，**

**[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)黑豆[童便](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.7.0.0.md)酒，消淤下胎痛逆忘。**

本方由[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，川芎，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，[黑姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.1.0.0.md)，炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等五味药组成。功能活血化淤，温经止痛。主治产后恶露不行，少腹冷痛。

黑神散由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)，归尾，赤芍，[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)，桂心，[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，黑豆等八味药组成主治产后、恶露不尽，攻冲作痛，胞衣不下或胎死腹中。

**7.失笑散**

**失笑五灵与[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)，晕平痛止效非常，**

**活血行淤散结痛，产后血滞此方尝。**

本方由[五灵脂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.22.0.0.md)，蒲赀两药组成。功能活血、祛淤、止痛。主治产后恶露不行，少腹急痛，甚则卒然晕倒，不省人事。

**8.通窍活血汤（附：血府逐淤汤、腩下逐淤汤、少腹逐淤汤〉**

**通窍全凭好[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)，桃红[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)老葱姜，**

**川芎黄酒赤芍药，表里通经第一方。**

**血府[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)生地桃，[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)壳赤芍，**

**[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)芎桔[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)等，血化下行不作劳。**

**膈下逐淤桃牡丹，赤芍[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)元胡甘，**

**归穹灵脂[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)売，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)开郁血亦安。**

**少腹[茴香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.9.0.0.0.md)与炒姜，元胡灵脂没芎当，**

**[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)官桂赤芍药，调经种子第一方。**

本方由赤芍，川芎，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)，老葱，鲜姜，鲜枣，[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)，黄酒组成。功能行淤通窍。主治头痛昏晕、耳聋、脱发、面青，以及妇人干血成痨，小儿疳积症。

血府逐淤汤甶[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)，枳売，赤芍，[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)，川芎，[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)等十三味药组成，功能破淤宽膈，行气止痛，主治血淤胸膈胸满隐痛，痛有定处而日久不愈，烦闷心悸，舌青口燥等症。

膈下逐淤汤由灵脂，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，川芎，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)，丹皮，赤芍，[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)，玄胡索，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[香附](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)，[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)等十二味药组成，功能行气破淤，活血止痛，主治膈大淤血之脘腹等痛或刺痛，痛处不移。

少腹逐淤汤由小[茴香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.9.0.0.0.md)，[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)，玄胡索，[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，川芎，官桂，赤芍，[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)，灵脂等十味药组成，功能活血袪淤，温经止痛，主治少腹刺痛，冷痛，痛而无块，亦治宫寒不孕。

**9.[复元活血汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx09-0.3.0.0.0.md)**

**[复元活血汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx09-0.3.0.0.0.md)[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)，花粉[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)山甲储，**

**[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)草，损伤淤血酒煎除。**

本方由[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)，[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)根，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，山甲，[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)等八味药组成。功能活血祛淤，疏肝通络。主治跌打损伤，胸胁淤肿疼痛难忍。

**10.七厘散**

**七厘散是伤科方，[血竭](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.15.0.0.0.md)[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)冰[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)。**

**乳没儿茶朱共末，酒调内服外敷良。**

本方由[血竭](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.15.0.0.0.md)，[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)，[冰片](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.3.0.0.md)，[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)，[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)，[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)，[朱砂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.1.0.0.md)，儿茶等八味药组成。功能活血散淤。主治跌打损伤，筋骨伤处肿胀疼痛。

**11.三甲散（《瘟疫论》）**

**山甲散治主客交，龟鳖山甲草归芍，**

**[牡蛎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.5.0.0.md)䗪虫僵[蝉蜕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.5.0.0.md)，正虚血结此方超。**

本方由[鳖甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.15.0.0.md)，龟甲，[穿山甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.15.0.0.md)，白[僵蚕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.8.0.0.md)，[牡蛎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.5.0.0.md)，[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，䗪虫，[蝉蜕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.5.0.0.md)等九味药组成。功能逐淤通脉。主治温病后，神识不清，默默不语之症。

### 【止血】

**12.十灰散**

**十灰散用十般灰，柏茅茜荷丹榈煨，**

**二蓟栀黄各炒黑，用此止血热势微。**

本方由大蓟，小蓟，[荷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.15.0.0.md)，[侧柏叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.2.0.0.md)，[茜草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.13.0.0.md)根，茅根，[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，山栀，[棕榈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.10.0.0.md)皮，[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)等十味药组成。功能凉血止血。主治呕血、咯血等热病失血之症。

**13.四生丸**

**四生丸用三般叶，侧柏艾荷生地协，**

**等分生捣如泥煎，血热妄行止衄愜。**

**愜** qie，读怯，恰当。

本方由生[荷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.15.0.0.md)，生[艾叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.15.0.0.md)，生柏叶，[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)等四味药捣和为丸而成。功能凉血止血。主治血热妄行所致的吐血、衄血。

**14.咳血方**

**咳血方中[诃子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.7.0.0.md)收，蒌海山栀力最优，**

**[青黛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.6.0.0.md)蜜丸口噙化，咳嗽痰血服之瘳。**

**噙** qin，读琴，含在口中。

本方由[青黛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.6.0.0.md)，[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)仁，[诃子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.7.0.0.md)，海石，山栀等五味药组成。功能清火止咳。主治咳嗽痰中带血，吐咯不爽，心烦口苦等症。

**15.[小蓟饮子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx09-0.5.0.0.0.md)**

**[小蓟饮子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx09-0.5.0.0.0.md)藕[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)，[木通](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.8.0.0.md)[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)生地囊，**

**归草黑栀[淡竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.22.0.0.md)，血淋热结服之良。**

木方由[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)，小蓟，[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)，[蒲黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.14.0.0.md)，[淡竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.22.0.0.md)，耦节，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，山栀，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)等十味药组成。功能凉血止血，利尿通淋。主治血淋尿血，小便频数，赤涩热痛。

**16.槐花散(附:槐角丸、脏连丸)**

**槐花散用治肠风，侧柏黑荆[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)充，**

**为末等分米饮下，宽肠凉血逐风功。**

**槐角丸亦治肠风，[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)归榆枳苓供，**

**更有脏连疗下血，猪肠[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)法当宗。**

本方出槐花，柏叶，[荆芥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.4.0.0.md)穗，[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)等四味药组成。功能疏风止血。主治痔疮出血。

槐角丸由[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)，[地榆](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.4.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，枳売，[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)等五味药组成，功能清肠止血，主治痔疮下血、脱肛。

脏连丸由[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)，猪大肠头两味药制成，亦治痔疮出血。

**17.[黄土汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx09-0.6.0.0.0.md)**

**[黄土汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx09-0.6.0.0.0.md)中术附苓，[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)地黄并，**

**便后下血功专擅，吐衄崩中效亦灵。**

本方由[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[干地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.3.0.0.md)，[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)，[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)，[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)，灶心黄土等七味药组成。功能温脾摄血。主治虚寒性便血、吐血、衄血及妇人月经过多等症。

**18.胶艾汤**

**胶艾汤中四物先，[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)[艾叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.15.0.0.md)草同煎，**

**妇人良方单胶艾，胎动能安腹痛全。**

本方由川芎，[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，[艾叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.15.0.0.md)，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，芍药，[干地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.3.0.0.md)等七味药组成。功能补血调经，止漏安胎。主治妇女月经不调，淋漓不净及胎漏等症。

## 16治风剂

### 【疏散外风】

**1.[小续命汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.9.0.0.0.md)（附:续命汤）**

**[小续命汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.9.0.0.0.md)桂附芎，[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)参芍杏[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)，**

**黄芩[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)兼姜草，风中诸经以此通。**

**除去[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)附芩芍，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)改作[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)充，**

**再加[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)与[石膏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.1.0.0.md)，风痱肢废有殊功。**

**风痱** 病名，痱与废义同，此处指中风后下肢瘫废。

本方由[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)、[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、桂心、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、芍药、川芎、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等十二味药组成，功能温经散寒，主治中风后半身不遂，兼有恶寒身痛之表症者。

本方去[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)，[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)易[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)，再加[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[石膏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.1.0.0.md)，名续命汤，功能散寒通痹，主治中风后下肢偏废。

**2.[大秦艽汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.1.0.0.0.md)**

**大[秦艽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.4.0.0.md)用羌独防，芎芷辛苓二地黄，**

**[石膏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.1.0.0.md)归芍苓甘术，疏散风邪可通尝。**

本方由[秦艽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[石膏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、川芎、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)等十六味药组成，功能散风清热，主治中风后手足不行，舌强不能言，兼有寒热症状者。

**3.三生饮（附:星香散，大省风汤，青州白丸子)**

**三生饮用乌附星，三药生用[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)听，**

**加参扶正宗薛氏，风痰卒中效颇灵。**

**若加[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)除乌附，专治咽喉痰上升。**

**大省风汤即三生，防蝎独草去香煎，**

**中风痰厥人昏倒，手足抽搐口潮涎。**

**青州白丸亦三生，再加[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)威力添，**

**晒露糊丸姜薄引，风痰瘫痪服之验。**

本方由生南星、生川岛、生[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)等四味药组成，功能温经散寒，理气化痰，主治中风后恶寒肢冷，痰气壅盛之症。薛立斋主张本方加[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)扶正，其效尤灵。

本方去川乌、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)，加[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、生南星，名星香散，功能降逆化痰，主治中风后痰壅气阻。

本方去[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，加[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[全蝎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、名大省风汤，功能祛风通痹，主治中风，猝然仆倒，眩晕痰多，四肢抽搐，并治历节痛。

青州白丸由三生饮去[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)易白[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)，再加[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)组成。主治中风手足抽描，口中涎痰多。

**4.[牵正](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.1.9.0.md)散**

**[牵正](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.1.9.0.md)散是杨家方，[全蝎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.9.0.0.md)[僵蚕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.8.0.0.md)白附襄，**

**服用小量热酒下，风中络脉疗效彰。**

木方由白[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[僵蚕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.8.0.0.md)、[全蝎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.9.0.0.md)等三味药组成，功能熄风化痰，主治面瘫，口眼歪斜。

**5.[独活寄生汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.11.0.0.0.md)（附：三痹汤，[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)[续断](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.xd.md)汤）**

**[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)寄生艽防辛，芎归地芍桂苓均，**

**[杜仲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.0.md)[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)草，冷风顽痹屈能伸。**

**若去寄生加芪续，汤名三痹古方珍。**

**或去独寄与[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，加羌续芷瘘痹行。**

**三痹**  指痛痹、行痹、着痹，此处作方名。

木方由[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[桑寄生](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[秦艽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，芍药、川芎、[干地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[杜仲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.0.md)、[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、桂心等十五味药组成，功能益肝肾、祛风湿、止痹痛，主治风湿痹症，腰膝冷痛，肢节屈伸不利，肌肉疼痛，麻木不仁，日久不愈。

本方去寄生，加[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[续断](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.10.0.xd.md)，名三痹汤，主治风寒湿痹，手足拘挛等症。

**6.蠲弊汤（附:舒筋汤，租氏蠲痹汤）**

**蠲痹汤医风气痹，羌防归芍共[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)，**

**[姜黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.4.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)姜煎服，体痛筋挛手足痱，**

**除去芪防加桐术，肩腰作痛使筋舒。**

**程氏蠲痹用桂羌，独艽芎归乳[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，**

**[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[桑枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.17.0.0.md)海风藤，风寒湿邪均能匡。**

本方由[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、[姜黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、赤芍、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等八味药组成，功能益气血、祛风湿，主治风痹、项背拘急，肌肉关节疼痛，游走不定。

本方去[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)，加[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[海桐皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.13.0.0.md)，名舒筋汤，功能健脾燥湿，主治肩背腰膝疼痛，手足麻木。

程氏蠲痹汤由[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、桂心、[秦艽](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、川芎、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、海风藤、[桑枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.17.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)等十一味药组成，功能活血通痹，主治风寒湿痹，久痛不愈。

**7.[玉真散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**[玉真散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.2.0.0.0.md)治破伤风，牙关紧急反张弓，**

**星麻白附羌防芷，外敷内服一方通。**

本方由南星、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、[天麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.6.0.0.md)、[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、白[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)等六味药组成，功能祛风止痉，主治破伤风，牙关紧闭，角弓反张。

**8.川芎茶调散**

**川芎茶调散荆防，辛芷[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)羌，**

**目昏鼻塞风攻上，偏正头痛悉平康。**

本方由[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、川芎、[荆芥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.4.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)等八味药组成，功能疏风止痛，主治头痛兼有恶寒发热身痛等症者。

**9.大活络丹（附：[小活络丹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.3.0.0.0.md)）**

**大活络丹五十味，三物四君为首位，**

**羌防辛葛桂黄麻，麻安丁木沉藿附。**

**附蔻青乌[血竭](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.15.0.0.0.md)研，乌连龙星[骨碎补](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.12.0.0.md)，**

**二蛇蚕蝎乳没尖，[牛黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.2.0.0.md)冰麝犀龟虎，**

**贯芩[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)何[首乌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.2.0.0.md)，灵仙松脂足其数。**

**[小活络丹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.3.0.0.0.md)用胆星，二乌乳没地龙寻，**

**酒丸酒下能通络，风血痰涎闭在经。**

大活络丹由五十味药物组成，即：[白花蛇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.8.0.0.md)、[乌梢蛇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[威灵仙](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.2.0.0.md)、两头尖、草乌、[全蝎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[首乌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.2.0.0.md)、龟板、[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)、贯仲、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、官桂、[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)、赤芍，[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)，[丁香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.8.0.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、姜虫、南星、[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[骨碎补](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.12.0.0.md)、[白豆蔻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[安息香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.6.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、香[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、[葛根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.8.0.0.md)、虎胫骨、梅片、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[血竭](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.15.0.0.0.md)、地龙、[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[麝香](https:// [小活络丹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.3.0.0.0.md)由川芎、草乌、地龙、南星、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)等六味药组成，功能活络止痛，主治中风后手足不仁和风湿痹痛，肢体麻木等症。

**10.着痹验方（《中医方剂临床手册》）**

**验方着痹蝎蜈吞，地鳖蛇蜂[虎骨](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.11.0.0.md)伸，**

**钻地老鹳蜣螂草，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)寻骨鹿衔斟，**

本方由[蜈蚣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.10.0.0.md)、[全蝎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.9.0.0.md)、蜣螂、蕲蛇、蜂房、[虎骨](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.11.0.0.md)、地鳖虫、寻骨风、伸筋草、钻地风、鹿衔草、老鹳草、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)等十三味药组成，功能搜风通络，主治风湿痹痛，痛处固定不移。

### 【平熄内风】

**小儿急惊牙关紧，手足抽搐效验卓。**

**撮风散向直[僵蚕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.8.0.0.md)，赤脚[蜈蚣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.10.0.0.md)朱麝全，**

**13.[大定风珠](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx16-0.7.0.0.0.md)（附：小定风珠）**

## **17祛湿剂**

### **【燥湿化浊】**

**1.[平胃散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.1.0.0.0.md)**（附：不换金正气散、柴平汤）

**[平胃散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.1.0.0.0.md)是[苍术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.2.0.0.md)朴，[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)四般药，**

**除湿散满驱瘴疬，调胃化湿此方速。**

**[平胃散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.1.0.0.0.md)内加夏藿，金不换来正气复。**

**[小柴胡汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx02-0.1.0.0.0.md)合平胃，寒多热少属湿疟。**

瘴疬zhang1i、读丈厉，山瘴瘟疬之气，为恶性疟疾之病源。

本方由[苍术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等四味药组成，功能健脾燥湿，主治舌腻，食不化，腹胀便溏等症。

本方加[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)，名不换金正气散，功能化浊和中，主治寒热呕吐，脘痞不食。

本方合[小柴胡汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx02-0.1.0.0.0.md)，名柴平汤，主治湿疟。

**2.六和汤**

**六和藿朴杏砂呈，[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)赤[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**参术扁豆同[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，姜枣煎之六气平。**

本方由[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、扁豆、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)等十一味药组成，功能和中祛暑，燥湿化浊，主治夏日舌苔厚浊，饮食不化、腹胀、呕吐泄泻等证。

**3.[藿香正气散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx02-0.3.0.0.0.md)**

**[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)正气腹皮苏，甘桔陈苓术朴俱，**

**夏曲[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)加姜枣，风寒暑湿并能驱。**

本方由[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[紫苏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.3.0.0.md)、[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、[大腹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等十一味药组成，功能解表和中，主治四时外感所致的呕吐、腹痛、泄泄等证。

### **【清热利湿】**

**4.[甘露消毒丹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.4.0.0.0.md)**

**甘露消毒蔻[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)，[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)[木通](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.8.0.0.md)菖，**

**芩翘[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)[射干](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.11.0.0.md)薄，暑疫湿温为未尝。**

本方由[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[石菖蒲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[木通](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.8.0.0.md)、川[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[射干](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.11.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)、白蔻仁、[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)等十一味药组成，功能清热化湿，主治舌苔黄腻，胸闷发热，尿短黄或发生黄疸等证。

**5.[三仁汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.3.0.0.0.md)**（附：藿朴夏苓汤）

**三仁杏蔻[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)，朴夏白通滑竹伦，**

**水用甘澜扬百遍，湿温初起法堪遵。**

**藿朴夏苓有三仁、[猪苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.3.0.0.md)[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)豆豉群，**

**主治湿温口不渴，胸闷口腻最有灵。**

本方由[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、生薏仁、白蔻仁、[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)等八味药组成，功能宣畅气机，清利湿热，主治湿热初起，舌白腻、胸闷发热，口不渴之证。

本方去[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.6.0.0.md)，加入[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)、豆豉、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[猪苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)，名藿朴夏苓汤，亦治湿温初起，身热不渴，肢体倦怠，胸闷口腻之证。

**6.连朴饮**

**连朴饮内用豆豉，菖蒲[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)炒山栀，**

**[芦根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.4.0.0.md)[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)入，湿热霍乱此方施。**

本方由[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[石菖蒲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、香豉、山栀、[芦根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.4.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能理气化浊，主治藿乱吐泻，胸闷痞满，小便短赤。

**7.二妙散**（附：三妙丸）

**二妙散中苍柏兼，若云三妙[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)添，**

**痿痹足疾堪多服，湿热全除病自痊。**

本方由[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[苍术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.2.0.0.md)二味药组成，功能清热燥湿，主治湿热痹证，关节肿痛、热痛，屈伸不便。

本方加[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)，名三妙散，亦治关节疼痛和腰膝胀痛。

**8.[茵陈蒿汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.2.0.0.0.md)**（附：栀予柏皮汤）

**[茵陈蒿汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.2.0.0.0.md)治黄疸，栀子[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)组成方。**

**栀子柏皮加[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，二方同属治阳黄。**

本方由[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)、栀子、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)三味药组成，功能清热利湿，主治湿热黄疸。

栀子柏皮汤由栀子、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)皮三味药组成，主治伤寒身热发黄。

**9.[八正散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.5.0.0.0.md)**（附：[石苇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.11.0.0.md)散、五淋散）

**八正[木通](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.8.0.0.md)与车前，扁蓄[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)研，**

**草梢[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)兼栀子，煎加[灯草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.21.0.0.md)效立见。**

**[石苇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.11.0.0.md)散用通车前，榆皮[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)赤[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**葵子[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)与[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)，主治茎痛砂石淋。**

**五淋散用栀子仁，赤芍[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)与[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)生用为细末，热结能除[水道](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.1.1-3-0.1.3.3.28.md)澄。**

本方由车前子、[木通](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.8.0.0.md)、[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)、扁蓄、[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、栀子、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、灯芯等九味药组成，功能清热泻火，利水通淋，主治热淋，尿频涩痛，淋沥不畅，少腹胀满，口干咽燥；亦治石淋，尿时茎中痛或有砂石。

本方去扁蓄、栀子、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，加[石苇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.11.0.0.md)、榆白皮、[冬葵子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.17.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、名[石苇](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.11.0.0.md)散，主治石淋、砂淋病。

五淋散由[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、赤芍、山栀等五味药组成，主治热淋、血淋、小便带血，淋漓涩痛。

**10.中满分消丸**（附：中满分消汤）

**中满分消砂朴姜，芩连夏陈知泽襄，**

**二苓参术[姜黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.4.0.0.md)草，[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)为丸效力彰。**

**又有中满分消汤，乌泽连参青归姜，**

**陈柴[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)茄益智，夏苓[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)与[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)，**

**吴萸[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)[草豆蔻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.6.0.0.md)，芪柏共煎中满匡。**

本方由[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[猪苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[姜黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[砂仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)等十六味药组成，功能燥湿清热，理气除胀，主治脘腹胀满，二便不利。

中满分消汤由川乌、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)、[荜澄茄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.10.1.0.0.md)、[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[青皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)、[草果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[益智仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.9.0.0.md)等二十一味药组成，功能补脾升阳，散寒理气，主治脏寒腹胀，暮夜其胀更甚。

**11.燃照汤**（《霍乱论》）

**燃照汤中省头草，朴蔻香豉肠胃保，**

**滑夏栀芩并清热，骤作好吐泻凉服。**

本方由[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)、[淡豆豉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.6.0.0.md)、焦山栀、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、佩兰、[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能清暑利湿，主治霍乱吐泻，脘痞烦渴。

**12.蚕矢汤**（《霍乱论》）

**蚕矢汤中用蚕砂，豆卷栀苡芩连夏，**

**湿热壅郁经络拘，还入吴萸通[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)。**

本方由蚕砂、[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)、大豆黄卷、[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)、焦栀、[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)等十味药组成，功能清热利湿，升清降浊，主治霍乱转筋，吐泻交作，并治骨节烦疼之痹痛。

**13.薏苡[竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.6.0.0.md)散**（《温病条辨》)

**薏苡[竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.6.0.0.md)治白㾦，通苓滑蔻翘草随。**

**汗多自利身热痛，辛凉淡泄法堪垂。**

白㾦 湿温病过程中于颈、项、胸腹皮肤所出现的一种细白水疱，状如水晶。

本方由[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[竹叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.6.0.0.md)、飞[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)、白蔻仁、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、白[通草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.9.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能清热利湿，主治发热身痛，汗多，腹泻，及胸腹部发生白㾦。

### **【利水化湿】**

**14.[五苓散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.6.0.0.0.md)**（附：四苓散，[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)[五苓散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.6.0.0.0.md)，胃苓汤）

**[五苓散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.6.0.0.0.md)治太阳腑，[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)[猪苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.3.0.0.md)茯，**

**[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)化气兼解表，小便通行水饮逐。**

**除却[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)名四苓，[五苓散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.6.0.0.0.md)加[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)助，**

**平胃五苓二散合，行气燥湿法兼顾。**

本方由[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[猪苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)等五味药组成，功能解表利水，主治小便不利，渴欲饮水，水入则吐及泄泻等症。

本方去[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)名四苓散，亦治小便不利，大便溏泻和水入则吐之证。

本方加[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)，名[茵陈](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.15.0.0.md)[五苓散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.6.0.0.0.md)，功能清热利湿，主治湿热黄疸。

本方合[平胃散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.1.0.0.0.md)，名胃苓汤，功能健脾利湿和中，主治湿滞伤食，脘腹胀满，腹痛泄泻。

**15.[猪苓汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.7.0.0.0.md)**

**[猪苓汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.7.0.0.0.md)内二苓全，[泽泻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.4.0.0.md)[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)添，**

**利水育阴兼泻热，溺秘心烦呕渴痊。**

本方自[五苓散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.6.0.0.0.md)去[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、加[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[滑石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.7.0.0.md)而成，功能滋阴利水，主治烦热，口渴欲饮，小便不利等证。

**16.五皮散**

**五皮散用五般皮，陈茯姜桑大腹奇，**

**或以五加易桑白，脾虚腹胀此方宜。**

本方由[桑白皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.6.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)皮、[大腹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)皮等五味药组成，功能利湿消肿，主治全身浮肿，小便不利之皮水证。

**17.[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)汤**（附：防已[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)汤）

**[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)金匮方，[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)枣[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)，**

**此疗风水与诸湿，汗出恶风身重尝。**

**方中去枣[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)姜，加入[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)良，**

**水在皮肤聂聂动，可用[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)汤，**

本方由[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[防己](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等六味药组成，功能健脾利水，主治水肿，风湿痹痛兼见汗出恶风、身重、小便不利者。

本方去[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，加[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，名防已[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)汤，主治水肿，兼四肢肌肉有波动状。

### **【温水化湿】**

**18.苓桂术甘汤**

**苓桂术甘蠲饮剂，崇脾以利膀胱气，**

**饮邪上逆[气冲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.1.1-3-0.1.3.3.30.md)胸，胸满能愈眩晕弃。**

本方由[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)四药组成，功能健脾逐饮，主治胸肋胀满，眩晕心悸，短气而咳等证。

**19.[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)汤**

**肾着汤内用[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)，[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)襄，**

**伤湿身痛腰冷重，亦名甘姜苓术汤。**

本方又名肾着汤，由苓桂术甘汤去[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)，加[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)而成，功能温脾胜湿，主治身重、身痛、腰冷痛。

**20.[实脾散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.9.0.0.0.md)**

**实脾苓术与[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)大腹加，**

**[草果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.7.0.0.md)姜附兼[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)，虚寒阴水效堪夸。**

本方由[厚朴](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[草果](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.7.0.0.md)、大腹子、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、白[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等十味药组成，功能温阳利水，主治全身水肿，半身以下更甚，胸满腹胀，身重食少，恶寒肢冷等症。

21. **蓖薢分清饮**（附：程氏[萆薢分清饮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.10.0.0.0.md)）

**蓖薢分清[石菖蒲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.5.0.0.md)，草梢[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)智仁俱，**

**或益[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)盐煎服，淋浊留连数剂除。**

**心悟蓖薢分清饮，清利湿热功效准，**

**蓖柏菖苓丹[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)，车前子与[莲子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.13.0.0.md)心。**

本方由[萆薢](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.14.0.0.md)、[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)、[石菖蒲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[益智仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.9.0.0.md)等四味药组成，功能分清化浊，主治膏淋、白浊，小便涩痛，淋漓不断，浑浊不清。

《医学心悟》所载之[萆薢分清饮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx10-0.10.0.0.0.md)，系前方减[益智仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.2.9.0.0.md)、[乌药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.6.0.0.md)，加[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[丹参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.7.0.0.md)、车前子、连子心等组成，亦治膏淋、白浊。

### **【宣散湿邪】**

**22.[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)胜湿汤**

**[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)胜湿羌独芎，蔓甘[藁本](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.8.0.0.md)与[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)，**

**湿邪在表头腰重，发汗升阳有异功。**

本方自[羌活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.6.0.0.md)、[独活](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[藁本](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.8.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、川芎、[蔓荆子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.7.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能祛风胜湿，主治风寒感冒及风湿痹痛。

**23.鸡鸣散**

**鸡鸣散是绝奇方，苏叶吴萸[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)姜，**

**瓜橘[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)煎冷服，肿浮脚气效验彰。**

本方由[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[木瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc06-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[吴茱萸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.5.0.0.0.md)、[紫苏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.3.0.0.md)叶、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能温化寒湿，主治寒湿痹痛及脚气病。

**24.五叶[芦根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.4.0.0.md)汤**（《温热病篇》）

**五叶[芦根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.4.0.0.md)化湿方，藿佩枇杷二荷汤，**

**芦尖瓜瓣轻芳化，湿热䝉蔽透清阳。**

本方由[藿香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc04-0.0.1.0.0.md)叶、[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)叶、[荷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[枇杷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.9.0.0.md)、佩兰叶、[芦根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[冬瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.18.0.0.md)仁等七味药组成，功能清利湿热，主治湿温病，身热已退，除邪朱净。

**25.[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)丸**（《金匮要略》）

**金匮[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)丸，[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)水气宣，**

**苦渴仍以[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)化，阴阳补泻此方全。**

本方由[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)根、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[瞿麦](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.12.0.0.md)等五药组成，功能温阳利水，主治小便不利，上有口渴，下见足冷。

## 18**润燥剂**

### **【轻宣润燥】**

**1.[杏苏散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**[杏苏散](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.2.0.0.0.md)内夏陈前，甘桔枳苓姜枣研，**

**轻宣温润治凉燥，服后微汗病自痊。**

本方由苏叶、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[前胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等十一味药组成，功能宣肺化痰，主治秋月新凉外感，发热咳嗽。

**2.桑杏汤**（附：翘荷汤〉

**桑杏汤用象贝宜，[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)栀豉与梨皮。**

**翘荷甘桔焦栀豆。清宣凉润燥能医。**

本方由[桑叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.3.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)、象贝、香豉、栀皮、梨皮等七味药组成，功能生津润肺，主治肺燥咳嗽，干咳痰少。

翘荷汤由[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、生[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、栀皮、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[绿豆](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.17.0.0.md)皮等七味药组成，功能清热养阴，主治身热口渴，干咳无痰，鼻干涩不适。

**3.[清燥救肺汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.1.0.0.0.md)**

**清燥救肺参草杷，[石膏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.1.0.0.md)胶杏麦[胡麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.16.0.0.md)，**

**经霜收下冬[桑叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.3.0.0.md)，清肺润燥效堪夸。**

本方由冬[桑叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.3.0.0.md)、[石膏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[胡麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.16.0.0.md)仁、[阿胶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.5.0.0.md)、麦冬、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[枇杷叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.9.0.0.md)等九味药组成，功能清燥润肺，主治心烦口渴，咽喉干燥，干咳无痰。

**4.[沙参麦冬汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx07-0.8.0.0.0.md)**

**[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)麦冬扁豆桑，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)玉粉合成方，**

**秋燥耗津伤肺胃，苔光干咳最堪尝。**

本方由[沙参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.1.0.0.md)、玉竹参、生[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、麦冬、冬[桑叶](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.3.0.0.md)、扁豆、[天花粉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.5.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能清润肺胃，主治咽干口渴，干咳少痰，舌红少苔等症。

**5.清咽栀豉汤**（《疫喉浅论《或《温病学》）

**热盛清咽栀豉汤，银翘蚕豉桔牛蒡，**

**[马勃](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.9.0.0.md)[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)栀犀草，透邪清里两解方。**

本方由山栀、豆豉、银花、[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)、[牛蒡子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.2.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)、白[僵蚕](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.8.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)壳、苦[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、蝉衣等十一味药组成，功能清利咽喉，主治发热、咳嗽痰多，咽喉肿痛。

**6.清咽养营汤**（《疫喉浅论》或《温病学》）

**余毒伤阴养营汤，甘苦合法增液汤，**

**天冬知芍[茯神](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.2.0.0.md)草，洋参花粉共煎尝。**

本方由西洋参、大生地、[茯神](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.2.0.0.md)、麦冬、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[天花粉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[天门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.3.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、炙[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等十味药组成，功能滋阴生津，主治烂喉痧后期烦热口渴，咳嗽咽痛。

### **【甘寒滋润】**

**7.琼玉膏**（附：臞仙琼玉膏）

**琼玉膏中[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)，参苓白蜜炼膏尝，**

**肺枯干咳虚劳证，金水相生效倍彰。**

**又有臞仙琼玉膏，原方加沈琥半两，**

**喉中血腥肠隐痛，嗜酒久咳效尤强。**

**臞**qu，读渠。义同“癯”，瘐。

本方由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、白[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、白蜜等四味药组成，功能养阴润肺，主治虚劳干咳，咽燥咯血。

本方加[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)、[琥珀](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.10.0.0.md)，名臞仙琼玉膏，功能润肺降逆，主治虛劳咳血，胸中隐痛。

**8.[百合固金汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.4.0.0.0.md)**

**[百合](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.7.0.0.md)固金二地黄，[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)甘桔藏，**

**麦冬芍药[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)配，喘咳痰血肺家伤。**

本方由[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、麦冬、[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[百合](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.7.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、芍药、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等十味药组成，功能滋阴润肺，主治咽喉燥痛，手足烦热，咳嗽气喘，痰中带血等症。

**9.[养阴清肺汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.3.0.0.0.md)**

**郑氏[养阴清肺汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.3.0.0.0.md)，[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)甘芍冬地黄，**

**[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)丹皮入，时疫白喉是妙方。**

本方由[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)、麦冬、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)、[白芍](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.4.0.0.md)等八味药组成，功能养阴清肺，主治白喉初起，发热，咽喉肿痛，鼻干唇燥等症。

**10.五汁饮**

**五汁饮用五般汁，梨麦藕荠苇根给，**

**或以蔗浆来易藕，甘寒救液合医律。**

本方由梨汁、[荸荠](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.16.0.0.md)汁、苇根汁、麦冬汁、藕汁等五药组成、功能生津润燥，主治温热病伤津，口干咽燥，干咳无痰，大便秘结等症。

**11.[麦门冬汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.5.0.0.0.md)**（附：加减[麦门冬汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.5.0.0.0.md)）

**[麦门冬汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.5.0.0.0.md)[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)参，枣甘粳米共合成，**

**咽喉不利因虚火，养胃除烦逆气平。**

**若于方中除粳米，[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)丹芍[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)增。**

本方由[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)、粳米等六味药组成，功能生津、降逆，主治咳唾涎沫，咽干，口燥，气短而喘之肺瘘。

原方去梗米，加[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、芍药、丹皮、[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)名加减[麦门冬汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx11-0.5.0.0.0.md)，主治妇女倒经，经期吐血、衄血等症。

**12.增液汤**

**增液汤用参地冬，滋阴生津大有功，**

**阳明温热肠燥结，水津四布大便通。**

本方由[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、麦冬、[生地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.2.0.0.md)三药组成，功能滋阴润肠，主治口渴，舌干红，大便秘结。

**13.[玉液](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.1.7.0.md)汤**（《医学衷中参西录》）

**[玉液](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.4-0.1.1.7.0.md)消渴方中珍，[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)芪葛[鸡内金](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.5.0.0.md)，**

**花粉知味滋兼敛，气升液至立意新。**

本方由生[山药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.6.0.0.md)、生[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[知母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.2.0.0.md)、生[鸡内金](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[葛根](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.8.0.0.md)、[五味子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[天花粉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.5.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能养阴益气，生治口渴尿多之消渴病。

## 19**祛痰剂**

### **【燥湿化痰】**

**1.[二陈汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx12-0.1.0.0.0.md)**（附：温胆汤、导痰汤、涤痰汤、金水六君煎）

**[二陈汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx12-0.1.0.0.0.md)用夏和陈，益以[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)臣，**

**利气调中兼去湿，一切痰饮此为珍。**

**若加[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)与[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)，汤名温胆可宁神，**

**导痰汤内加星枳，顽痰胶固力能驯。**

**涤痰汤用[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)星，[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)橘红参[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)菖蒲兼[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)，痰迷舌强服之醒。**

**金水六君用二陈，再加熟地与归身，**

**肺肾阴虚兼有痰，滋阴化痰效频灵。**

本方由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、橘红、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等四味药组成，功能燥湿化痰，主治咳嗽，胸闷痰多。

原方加[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)、[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)，名温胆汤，功能化痰除烦，主治眩晕，胸闷欲呕，虚烦不得眠。

本方加南星、[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)，名导痰汤，功能燥湿豁痰，主治咳嗽痰多，眩晕胸闷等症。

涤痰汤由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、胆星、橘红、[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、菖蒲、[竹茹](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)等十一味药组成，功能涤痰开窍，主治中风神识不清，舌强不语。

金水六君煎由[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能养阴祛痰，主治肺肾阴虚，湿痰内盛之证。

**2.指迷[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)丸**

**指迷[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)丸[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)，风硝[枳壳](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)姜汤下，**

**[中脘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.2.1-0.1.1.3.11.md)停痰肩臂疼，脉来沈细留心把。**

本方由[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、风化硝等四味药组成，功能消痰通络，主治痰停[中脘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/zjs/zjs3.2.1-0.1.1.3.11.md)，两臂酸痛。

### **【润燥化痰】**

**3.[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)散**（附：程氏[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)散）

**[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)散[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，橘[红花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.11.0.0.md)桔共煎成，**

**呛咳哽痛咽喉燥，润燥化痰奏效频。**

**程氏散中除[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，花粉[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)加连芩，**

**山栀胆星[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)组，主治类风痰热盛。**

本方由[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)、花粉、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、橘红、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)等六味药组成，功能润燥化痰。主治呛咳气喘、咽喉干燥。

本方去花粉、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、加[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、山栀、胆星、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，名程氏[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)散。治痰热壅盛之眩晕欲倒，心悸失眠之证。

### **【清热化痰】**

**4.清气化痰丸**

**清气化痰星夏橘，[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)实，**

**芩苓姜汁为糊丸，气顺火消痰自失。**

本方由[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[杏仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)、南星等八味药组成，功能清热化痰。主治发热咳嗽，口渴痰稠。

**5.小陷胸汤**（附：[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)陷胸汤）

**小陷胸汤连夏蒌，宽胸开结涤痰优，**

**脉浮滑兮按之痛，不按自疼大陷求。**

**[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)陷胸汤合成，气化痰热功颇灵，**

**除却[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)甘[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，加实桔连[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)仁。**

本方由[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)实等三味药组成，功能清热化痰，宽胸散结。主治咳嗽痰稠，胸脘痞满作痛。

[小柴胡汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx02-0.1.0.0.0.md)去[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[大枣](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.9.0.0.md)，加[枳实](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.3.0.0.md)、[桔梗](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[瓜蒌](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.4.0.0.md)仁，名[柴胡](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.9.0.0.md)陷胸汤。治往来寒热、呕恶胸痞。

**6.滚痰丸**（附：[竹沥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.6.0.0.md)达痰丸）

**滚痰丸用青[礞石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.9.0.0.md)，[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)辑，**

**诸证多因痰作怪，顽痰固结可消失。**

**[竹沥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.6.0.0.md)达痰滚痰丸，沉礞[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)及[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)，**

**[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)橘夏[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)草，姜汁[竹沥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.6.0.0.md)虚痰匡。**

本方由[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[礞石](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.9.0.0.md)、[沉香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.9.0.0.md)四药组成，功能降火祛痰。主治痰壅气急，眩晕欲呕，脉弦滑而数等证。

本方加[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[竹沥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.6.0.0.md)、[生姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.13.0.0.md)汁，名[竹沥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.6.0.0.md)达痰丸，功能固本逐痰，主治胸闷痰多，食少倦怠。

### **【祛寒化痰】**

**7.冷哮丸**

**皂杏半曲甘紫款，痰结冷喘此方珍。**

**9.[半夏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.1.0.0.md)[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)[天麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc10-0.0.6.0.0.md)汤**
