## **20驱虫剂**

**1.[乌梅丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx14-0.1.0.0.0.md)**

**[乌梅丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx14-0.1.0.0.0.md)用[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)桂，[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)椒姜继，**

**[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)及[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)，温脏安蛔寒厥剂。**

本方由[乌梅](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[细辛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.9.0.0.md)、[干姜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.4.0.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[川椒](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.7.0.0.0.md)、[桂枝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.2.0.0.md)、[黄柏](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)等十味药组成，功能温脏、安蛔。主治蛔厥、烦闷呕吐，腹痛腋冷。

**2.理中安蛔汤**

**理中方内有安蛔，姜术参苓椒之梅，**

**呕吐胃寒胸膈痛，温脾扶土去虫灾。**

本方由理中汤去[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)，加[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[川椒](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.7.0.0.0.md)、[乌梅](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.5.0.0.md)等药组成，功能温中安蛔。主治胸膈闷痛，呕吐不食，肢冷吐蛔之证。

**3.[肥儿丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx14-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**[肥儿丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx14-0.2.0.0.0.md)内用使君，豆蔻香连曲麦槟，**

**猪胆为丸热水下，疳虫积食尽离身。**

本方由[神曲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc14-0.0.4.0.0.md)、川连、[肉豆蔻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc18-0.0.6.0.0.md)、[使君子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.1.0.0.md)、去牙、[槟榔](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc15-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[木香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.5.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能消积驱虫。主治小儿虫积腹痛。

## 21**痈疡剂**

### **【痈疡阳证】**

**1.[仙方活命饮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.1.0.0.0.md)**（附：冲和汤）

**仙方活命[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)，防芷归陈草芍加，**

**[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)花粉兼乳没，穿山皂刺酒煎嘉，**

**—切痈疽能溃散，溃后忌服用毋差。**

**冲和汤用术归芪，参陈苓芎皂[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)，**

**乳没银花[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)节，酒水各半煎服宜，**

**半阴半阳疮疡正，似溃非溃效力奇。**

本方由[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)、[防风](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.5.0.0.md)、赤芍、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)尾、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)节、[皂角刺](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.17.0.0.md)、[穿山甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[天花粉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、银花、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)等十四味药组成，功能清热解毒，消肿溃坚。主治疮痈肿毒，已溃者忌用。

冲和汤由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[陈皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc11-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、川芎、[皂角刺](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.17.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、银花、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)节等十三味药组成，功能和营消肿。主治痈疮似溃非溃，没肿无头之证。

**2.银花解毒汤**（附：五味消毒饮)

**银花解毒地丁翘，[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)丹皮赤苓饶，**

**更用川连[夏枯草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.7.0.0.md)，痈疽疔毒服之消。**

**五味消毒疗诸疔，银花野菊蒲公英，**

**[紫花地丁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.4.0.0.md)天葵子，煎加酒服勿看轻。**

本方由[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)、地丁、[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)、赤[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、丹皮、[黄连](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.2.0.0.md)、[夏枯草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.1.7.0.0.md)等八味药组成，功能清热解毒，主治痈肿疔疮，坚硬热痛。

五味消毒饮由[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)、野菊花、蒲公英、[紫花地丁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.4.0.0.md)、紫背天葵等五味药组成，主治一切疔疮火毒。

**3.[犀黄丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.3.0.0.0.md)**（附：醒消丸）

**[犀黄丸](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.3.0.0.0.md)内用[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)，[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)与[牛黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.2.0.0.md)，**

**乳岩流注肠痈等，正气末虚均可尝。**

**醒消丸治红肿毒，乳没[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)雄精逐，**

**米饭为丸菔子大，服用酒送效力速。**

本方山[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、[牛黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.2.0.0.md)等五味药组成，功能解毒散结。主治乳癌、瘰疬、痰核和流注。

本方去[犀角](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.1.0.0.md)，加[雄黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.1.0.0.0.md)，名醒消丸，主治红肿痈毒。

**4.蟾酥丸**

**蟾酥丸用寒水石，麝朱乳没[胆矾](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc19-0.0.3.0.0.md)枯，**

**[轻粉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.5.0.0.0.md)铜绿雄蜗入，疔毒内服又外敷。**

本方由蟾酥、[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、铜绿、枯矾、[胆矾](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc19-0.0.3.0.0.md)、寒水石、蜗牛、[朱砂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[雄黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[轻粉](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.5.0.0.0.md)等十二味药组成，功能解毒散结。消肿止痛，主治痈肿、疔疮及疔毒内陷而致神昏。本方既可内服，亦可外敷。

**5.牛蒡解肌汤**

**牛蒡解肌[石斛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.4.0.0.md)丹，夏枯[荆芥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.4.0.0.md)[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)餐，**

**[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)栀子[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)入，风热疮疡勿等闲。**

本方由[牛蒡子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.2.0.0.md)、[薄荷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.1.0.0.md)、[荆芥](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.4.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、山栀、丹皮、[石斛](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.4.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、夏枯球等九味药组成，功能疏风消肿。主治头面风热，颈项肿毒，风热牙痛。

**6.五神汤**

**五神汤用紫地丁，[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)车前白[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**银花三两水煎服，湿热痈疮功可钦。**

本方由[茯苓](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.1.0.0.md)、车前子、[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)、[牛膝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.21.0.0.md)、[紫花地丁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.4.0.0.md)等五味药组成，功能清热解毒，主治下肢丹毒、痈疮。

**7.消瘰丸**

**消瘰丸用贝牡参，解郁化痰阴气增，**

**瘰疬津虚痰火结，加减临时细酌斟。**

本方由[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[牡蛎](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc09-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[贝母](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.2.3.0.0.md)三味药组成，功能化痰软坚。主治瘰疬、痰核。

**8.透脓散**（附：程氏透脓散、代刀散、托里透脓汤)

**透脓散治毒成脓，服此能成速溃功，**

**川芎归芪甲片皂，加芷蒡银效力雄，**

**去芎归甲加乳草，方名代刀力无穷。**

**托里透脓参术芷，[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)与皂刺，**

**[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)青麻[穿山甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.15.0.0.md)，痈疽发背用最宜。**

本方由生[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[穿山甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.15.0.0.md)、川芎、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[皂角刺](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.17.0.0.md)等五味药组成，功能补气透脓。主治痈疡，已成脓而不易溃破者。

本方去川芎、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、山甲，加[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)名代刀散，亦治痈疮成脓不溃。

托里透脓散由[人参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[白术](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.5.0.0.md)、[穿山甲](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.15.0.0.md)、[白芷](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.7.0.0.md)、[升麻](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.2.10.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)节、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、生[黄芪](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.4.0.0.md)、[皂角刺](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.17.0.0.md)、靑皮等十味药组成，功能益气养血，托里透脓。主治痈疮亏损，将溃之时毒气内陷。

### **【痈疡阴证】**

**1.[阳和汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.2.0.0.0.md)**

**[阳和汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.2.0.0.0.md)法解寒凝，外证虚寒色属阴，**

**熟地鹿胶姜炭桂，[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)白芥草相承。**

本方由[熟地黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.1.0.0.md)、[白芥子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc16-0.1.4.0.0.md)、鹿胶、[肉桂](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.3.0.0.0.md)、姜炭、[麻黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc01-1.1.1.0.0.md)、生[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等七味药组成，功能温阳散寒，宣发透毒。主治阴疽，色白，日久不能成脓外溃者。

**2.小金丹**

**小金丹内白胶香，木鳖地龙乳[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)，**

**归没五灵草乌墨，流注瘰疬服之良。**

本方由白胶香、草乌、灵脂、地龙、[木鳖子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc20-0.14.0.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[麝香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc08-0.0.1.0.0.md)、墨炭等十味药组成，功能散淤消肿。主治流注阴疽，痰核瘰疬及寒性疮疡。

### **【内痈】**

**1.[苇茎汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.4.0.0.0.md)**

**[苇茎汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.4.0.0.0.md)方出千金，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)薏苡[冬瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.18.0.0.md)仁，**

**淤热肺脏成痈毒，甘寒清热上焦宁。**

本方由苇茎、[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[冬瓜](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.18.0.0.md)仁、[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)等四味药组成，功能清肺壅。主治肺痈发热，咳嗽胸痛吐痰腥臭。

**2.[大黄牡丹汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.5.0.0.0.md)**（附: 清肠饮、红藤煎）

**金匮[大黄牡丹汤](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/fjx/fjx17-0.5.0.0.0.md)，[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)瓜子[芒硝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.2.0.0.md)襄，**

**肠痈初起腹按痛，尚末成脓服之康。**

**清肠饮用[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)，玄芩麦榆归草加，**

**苡仁五钱为煎剂，肠痈腹痛效不差。**

**红藤煎用[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)，红藤乳没翘索佳，**

**[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)丹皮地丁草，肠痈脓肿可代茶。**

本方由[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[桃仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.10.0.0.md)、瓜子、[芒硝](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.2.0.0.md)等五味药组成，功能泄热破淤，散结消肿。主治肠痈初起未溃。

清肠饮由[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[黄芩](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.2.1.0.0.md)、[麦门冬](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[地榆](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc13-0.0.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等八味药组成，功能清热解毒。主治肠痈腹痛甚，手不可按。

红藤汤由红藤、[紫花地丁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.4.0.0.md)、[乳香](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.13.0.0.md)、[没药](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.14.0.0.md)、[连翘](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.2.0.0.md)、[大黄](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc02-0.1.1.0.0.md)、[延胡索](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc12-0.0.2.0.0.md)、[牡丹皮](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.5.0.0.md)、[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等十味药组成，亦治肠痈。

**3.薏苡[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)败酱散**

**薏苡[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)败酱散，主治肠痈毒可斩。**

**肌肤甲错腹皮急，排脓消肿方堪赞。**

本方由[薏苡仁](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc05-0.0.5.0.0.md)、[附子](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc07-0.1.0.0.0.md)、[败酱草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.7.0.0.md)三味药组成，功能排脓消痈。主治肠痈已成脓而肌肤粗糙，腹部按之濡者。

**4.四妙勇安汤**（《验方新编》）

**四妙勇安治脱疽，银玄归草合用宜。**

**清热解毒兼活血，可疗红肿溃淋漓。**

本方由[金银花](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.4.1.0.0.md)、[玄参](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc03-0.3.4.0.0.md)、[当归](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.3.3.0.0.md)、[甘草](https://www.gmzyjc.com/read/bc/bc17-0.1.8.0.0.md)等四味药组成，功能解毒、活血。主治脱疽红肿溃烂。（何耀荣）
